in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在2004年的每一次大災難中 , 海嘯發生在巴基斯坦 , 2005年 , 85 , 000人死亡 , 海地地地震 , 大約有三十萬人死亡 , 最近發生的地震混合 , 讓日本和核融合 , 在所有這些情況下 , 我們看到國際演員、國際演員、國際間的合作關係 , 和國際間的合作 , 共同合作 , 來處理這種災難 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些是開源安全的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們把它們綁在一起 , 漸漸地 , 做這樣的事 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在你看到這個想法: 「 啊 , 道德 , 這些一定是溝通的海道 , 或這些可能是纖維電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 , 這是世界的圖表 , 根據推特 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 。 綠色是地理工程 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	人口調查的完美演化 , 世界上六大國家的下降順序:中國、印度、印度、臉書、美國、推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們要進入這些蚊帳 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	為什麼我們要參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們先前提到阿拉伯之春 , 以及所有這些力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉另一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦做了這樣的演講 。 我跟你們說 , 我在facebook上 。 朋友 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	聽眾笑了 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章 , 叫做ap , 在電線上 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	世界上有兩個地方 , 芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:南托米德需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	這個故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上 , 我有數百個臉書朋友 , 來自印尼人和芬蘭 , 說: 「 我們聽到你需要一個朋友 , 喔 , 順便說一下 , 納托是什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	沒錯 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何移動訊息 , 讓訊息傳遞給國際、國際間、私人和這些社交網絡 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我按下一個音符 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭警衛 。
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在helmand的手錶 , 位在南阿富汗 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他帶到這裡提醒我們 , 我不希望任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要有能力、競爭的軍隊 , 能創造出真正的軍事效應 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	那就是我們和我們所做的事的核心 , 我們要保護自由、言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍視的事物 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但你知道 , 生命不是一個大開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要軍隊 , 不論是在艱苦的戰役 , 或在巴拉克 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會主張 , 生命是個環節 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須把它放進去 , 如我所想的 , 在21世紀 , 我們在真實戰爭和危機中 , 將來會遇到困難的力量 , 但在現今我們談到的 , 軍隊可以創造出21世紀的安全、國際的、私人的、私人的、私人的、和人的溝通 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	我最後會說 , 我們早先聽過維基百科 。 我常常用維基百科 , 來尋找事實 , 如同你們所知 , 維基百科並不是十二個傑出的人在寫文章中創造出來的 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天都有數萬人輸入資訊 , 每一天 , 數百萬人戒斷這些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	對根本的意義來說 , 沒有人像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個盟友 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有一個人像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的願景很簡單:每個人都可以自由地分享所有知識的世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 藉由結合國際、介入、私人和戰略溝通 , 在21世紀 , 我們就能創造出所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常謝謝 。 謝謝 。
